| <span data-ttu-id="52d56-692">Ввод</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52d56-692">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52d56-693">Значение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52d56-693">Value</span></span> |
